The hotel will arrange a car to pick you up at the main entrance of the scenic area. Then after arriving at the East Gate, it is particularly convenient. As long as you book a room, you can directly report your reservation name to enter the park to avoid the frustration of queuing. A ticket will be issued to you at the door. After entering the park, you can check in at the hotel with the ticket. Friends who don‚Äôt drive can ask the hotel staff at the door to call a car to the hotel lobby. Walking into the lobby, the majestic Guanyin statue comes into view, plus the lotus pond in the lobby, carp spraying water, blue sky, white clouds, red flowers and Guanyin statues have a fairyland feeling. In the afternoon of check-in, go to the park where you want to take the sightseeing bus first, and you can continue to take the free battery car to the scenic spot the next day. It‚Äôs super convenient! Because the hotel is in the scenic area, you can enter and exit unlimited times without tickets during your stay. One room is free of 2 tickets, which is equivalent to directly saving 240 yuan in ticket money, and includes 2 people‚Äôs breakfast (breakfast is rich), which is really a good deal! Because it is off-season, the hotel has upgraded the room type, so you can see Guanyin Bodhisattva from the balcony of the guest room. The facilities are much better than before, with new decorations and new rooms, but I personally can accept it. The best thing is that you can enter the scenic area before the first wave of tourists arrive. The hotel's ferry can take guests to the square of the scenic area. It only takes about 10 minutes to walk from this location to the foot of Nanhai Guanyin. And hotel guests can enter the main hall without queuing. When you finish worshipping and hold the Buddha's feet, you will find that it is really worth it, because at this time the tourists outside have just come in and lined up in a long line! ! !
